<script type="text/javascript">    
   
    $(document).ready(function () {
        
        var SearchURL, Qry,temp;
        
        $(".icon-search, .search__btn").click(function () {
            try {
                console.log('Enter click event');
                //temp = $("#searchInput").val();
                temp = $("input[id$='searchInput']").val();
                if (temp != "") {
                    SearchURL = $("input[id$='URL']").val();
                    document.location = SearchURL + "?q=" + URLEncode(temp);
                }
            }
            catch (e) {
                console.log(e);
            }
        });
       
    });

    

    function URLEncode (clearString) {
        //debugger;
        var output = '';      
        var x = 0;       
        clearString = clearString.toString();      
        var regex = /(^[a-zA-Z0-9_.]*)/;
      
        while (x < clearString.length) {
           
            var match = regex.exec(clearString.substr(x));          
            if (match != null && match.length > 1 && match[1] != '') {
               
                output += match[1];               
                x += match[1].length;
              
            } else {
               
                if (clearString[x] == ' ')                   
                output += '+';
             
            else {
          
                var charCode = clearString.charCodeAt(x);               
                var hexVal = charCode.toString(16);               
                output += '%' + ( hexVal.length < 2 ? '0' : '' ) + hexVal.toUpperCase();               
            }           
            x++;          
        }       
    }  
    return output;
    }
</script>

        <script type="text/javascript">


            $(document).ready(function () {

                $("select[id$=ddlLanguages],select[id$=ddlCountries] ").bind('focus', function () {
                    if ($(this).closest('.frm__control').hasClass('has-error')) {
                        $(this).closest('.frm__control').removeClass('has-error');
                    }
                });
                
                RMChkBind();
          


                var jet_http_referrer = 'false';
                var ck = getCookie("pinStormId");

                if (jet_http_referrer == "true" && (ck == null || ck == "" || ck == undefined)) {
                    $.post("/JQueryAddUserControl.aspx",
                            { ClickedControl: "CreateSEOCookie", Jet_Referrer: '' },
                    function (data) { }
                    );
                    }

                var ddlCountries = $('#IWOVID_item_1_ddlCountries');
                var ddlLanguages = $('#IWOVID_item_1_ddlLanguages');
                var chkRememberMe = $('#IWOVID_item_1_chkRememberMe');
                var btnGo = $('#IWOVID_item_1_btnGo2');
                function RedirectURL(postControl) {
                    $.get("/JQueryAddUserControl.aspx",
                    {
                        ClickedControl: postControl,
                        Countries: ddlCountries.val(),
                        Languages: ddlLanguages.val(),
                        RememberMe: chkRememberMe.prop('checked')
                    }, function (data) {
                        var redirectURL = data;
                        var redirectURLSplit = redirectURL.split('$^');

                        if (redirectURLSplit[0] == "RedirectGetMethod") {
                            window.location.href = redirectURLSplit[1];
                        }
                        else if (redirectURLSplit[0] == "RedirectPostMethod") {
                        }

                    });
                    return false;
                };

                btnGo.click(function () {

                    if (ddlLanguages.val() == "" || ddlCountries.val() == "") {
                        if (ddlLanguages.val() == "") {
                            var holdLang = $("span[id$='errChooseLang']");
                            $(holdLang).closest('.frm__control').addClass('has-error');
                            $(holdLang).text("Please select language.");
                        }
                        else {
                            var holdCnty = $("span[id$='errChooseCountry']");
                            $(holdCnty).closest('.frm__control').addClass('has-error');
                            $(holdCnty).text("Please select country.");
                        }
                        return false;
                    }
                    else {
                        if (document.getElementById("LadingPageSubmitState").value == "true") {
                            if (typeof parseInt(ddlCountries.val()) == "number") {
                                RedirectURL('GoLandingPage')
                            }
                            return false;
                        }
                    }
                });

            });

            var rmCookie = "";
            var currCookie = "";
            function RMChkBind() {                
                var isRmSame = "false";
                var rmlangcountry = new Array();
                var currlangcountry = new Array();

                rmCookie = getCookie("CurrentSiteInfoRm");
                currCookie = getCookie("CurrentSiteInfo");

                
                if (rmCookie != null || rmCookie != undefined) {
                    rmlangcountry = getCountryLanguageCode(rmCookie);
                }
                else {
                }

                if (currCookie != null || currCookie != undefined) {

                    currlangcountry = getCountryLanguageCode(currCookie);
                }
                                
                if ((rmlangcountry.length > 0) && (currlangcountry.length>0))
                {
                    if (rmlangcountry[0] == currlangcountry[0] && rmlangcountry[1] == currlangcountry[1]) {
                        isRmSame = "true";
                    }
                    else {
                        isRmSame = "false";
                    }
                }

                if (isRmSame == "true") {
                    $("input[id$='chkRememberMe']").prop('checked', true);
                }
                else {
                    $("input[id$='chkRememberMe']").prop('checked', false);
                }

            }

            function getCountryLanguageCode(arrCountryLanguage) {
                var CountryLanguage = new Array();
                var language = ""; var country = "";
                arrCountryLanguage = arrCountryLanguage.split('&');
                for (var i = 0; i < arrCountryLanguage.length; i++) {
                    if (arrCountryLanguage[i].indexOf('LC') > -1) {
                        language = (arrCountryLanguage[i].split('=')[1]);
                    }
                    if (arrCountryLanguage[i].indexOf('COC') > -1) {
                        country = (arrCountryLanguage[i].split('=')[1]);
                    }
                }
                CountryLanguage[0] = language;
                CountryLanguage[1] = country;
                return CountryLanguage;
            }


            function getlanguage() {
                var ddlCountry = '#IWOVID_item_1_ddlCountries';
                var ddlLanguage = '#IWOVID_item_1_ddlLanguages';
                $.post("/JQueryAddUserControl.aspx",
                    {
                        ClickedControl: "GetLanguages",
                        CountryId: $(ddlCountry).val()
                    }, function (data) {
                        $(ddlLanguage + ">option").remove();
                        if (data != '') {
                            var lstLanguages = JSON.parse(data)
                            if (lstLanguages.length > 1)
                                $(ddlLanguage).append($('<option></option>').val("").html("---Choose Your Language---"));
                            for (var i = 0; i < lstLanguages.length; i++) {
                                $(ddlLanguage).append($('<option></option>').val(lstLanguages[i].LanguageID).html(lstLanguages[i].LanguageName));
                            }

                        }
                    });

            }



        </script>

        <script type="text/javascript">


            var setRememberMeCookie = function () {

                if (document.getElementById("IWOVID_item_1_chkRememberMe").checked == true)
                    setCookieEnableDisable('CurrentSiteInfoRm', 'true');
                else
                    setCookieEnableDisable('CurrentSiteInfoRm', '', -1);
            }

        </script>

<script type="text/javascript">


    //************* auth0 call*************
    
    var authorizationErrorDescription = '';    
    var IsSSOLogin = 'true';
    var SSOEnrollCall = false;
    
    var defaultCallbackUrl = 'http://www.jetairways.com/LoginCallback.ashx?state=ru%3d%2fEN%2fIN%2fJetPrivilege%2faccount-summary.aspx';

    if (IsSSOLogin == undefined || IsSSOLogin == '' || IsSSOLogin != "true")
    { IsSSOLogin = "false"; logconsole('exsiting Login call'); }

    if(document.location.pathname.replace('-','').toLowerCase().indexOf('enrolnow') > -1 ){
        var defaultCallbackUrl = 'http://www.jetairways.com/LoginCallback.ashx?state=ru%3d%2fEN%2fIN%2fJetPrivilege%2faccount-summary.aspx&enrollcall=y';
        SSOEnrollCall = true;
    }

    var auth0 = new Auth0({
        domain: 'sso.jetprivilege.com',
        clientID: 'mdMcEV7xNLkMxprupu7NfdvVqXoWRycs',
        callbackURL: defaultCallbackUrl
    });

    var AUTH0_CONNECTION = 'CRIS';
    var IsPFVStatus= '';
    var IsFlagSiteRegistered= '';

    // common Auth0 scripts for the site

    jQuery.deparam = function (params) {
        var o = {};
        if (!params) return o;
        var a = params.split('&');
        for (var i = 0; i < a.length; i++) {
            var pair = a[i].split('=');
            o[decodeURIComponent(pair[0])] = decodeURIComponent(pair[1]);
        }
        return o;
    }



    function configureunauthorizeduser() {
        // populate input with the username attempted when an authorization error occurred
        var authorizationErrorUsername = '';
        if (authorizationErrorUsername.length > 0) {
            input.val(authorizationErrorUsername);
        }
    }

    function configureRememberMe(checkbox, input) {
        logconsole('configureRememberMe');
        $.cookie.raw = true;
        var persistCookie = $.cookie('JPNumberRM');
        $.cookie.raw = false;

        var rememberMe = true; // default if no cookie
        if (persistCookie) {
            // cookie exists - parse out remember me value
            persistCookie = $.deparam(persistCookie);
            rememberMe = 'True';
        }

        checkbox.prop('checked', rememberMe);
        if (rememberMe) {
            input.val('');
    }
}

// attemptLogin
// - Performs an auth0.login() and retries if specific errors occur
// - Retry time intervals double with each attempt
// - A max of 5 retries is performed
function attemptLogin(interval, numTries, options, callback) {    
    logconsole('Performing login attempt: time interval=' + interval + 'ms, retry count=' + numTries);

    function handleError(err, callback) {   // consider displaying a more friendly error message
        //if (window.console) {
        //    console.error('An unexpected error occurred calling Auth0:', err);  
        //}         //logconsole('An unexpected error occurred calling Auth0:'+ err);
        
        if( err != undefined && err.message != undefined && err.message != '' && err.message.replace(' ','').toLowerCase().indexOf('unknownerror')!= -1){            
            ShowSSOLoginErrorMessage('An unexpected error occurred while logging you in.\nMake sure you are connected to the internet and try again.');
        }
        else{
            ShowSSOLoginErrorMessage(err.message); 
        }

        /*
        //logconsole('rinku '+err.message);
        if(err && err.message !=undefined  && err.message!='' && err.message.toLowerCase() !='undefined error')
        {        ShowSSOLoginErrorMessage(err.message);        }
        else{      ShowSSOLoginErrorMessage('An unexpected error occurred while logging you in.\nMake sure you are connected to the internet and try again.');}
        */
        if (callback) callback(err);
    }
    
    auth0.login(options, function (err) {

        
        // we only get here if there was an error; success results in a redirect
        
        // determine whether or not we can retry
        if (err.status === 500 && /^The script timed out/.test(err.message)) {
            if (numTries === 5) {
                // we've reached the max # of retries
                var err = new Error('The Auth0 service did not respond after the max number of retries.');
                handleError(err, callback);
            } else {
                // perform retry after time interval
                setTimeout(function () {
                    // double the time interval and increment the try count for the next retry
                    attemptLogin(interval * 2, numTries + 1, options, callback);
                }, interval);
            }
        } else {            
            // we've encountered a different error and can't retry
            handleError(err, callback);
        }
    });
}

function auth0Login(username, password, rememberMe, callback) {
    
    var options = {
        username: username,
        password: password,
        connection: AUTH0_CONNECTION,
        scope: 'openid profile'
    };
    
    if (rememberMe) {
        options.callbackURL = defaultCallbackUrl + '&remember=' + username;
    }    

    options.callbackURL = defaultCallbackUrl + '&JPN=' + username;
        
    attemptLogin(1000, 0, options, callback);
}

    function getCookie(JetUserInfo) {
        if (document.cookie.length > 0) {
            c_start = document.cookie.indexOf(JetUserInfo + "=");

            //c_start=document.cookie
            if (c_start != -1) {
                c_start = c_start + JetUserInfo.length + 1;
                c_end = document.cookie.indexOf(";", c_start);
                if (c_end == -1) c_end = document.cookie.length;
                return unescape(document.cookie.substring(c_start, c_end));
            }
        }
        return "";
    }

        function GetBestFares(citycode, senderTab) {
            JET.booking.getBestfare(citycode, senderTab);
        }

        function BindRVOBECookie() {            
            pastCookie = getCookie("RVOBECookie");
            JetUserCookie = getCookie("JetUserInfo");

            if (JetUserCookie == null || JetUserCookie == "") {
                var stdate = "";
                var endate = "";
                if (pastCookie == null || pastCookie == "") {
                }
                else {
                    stringToShow += "<h3>" + $("label[id$='lblpastSrchMsg']").html() + "</h3>"
                    stringToShow += "<ul class='airport-list past-searches'>";
                    pastSearchSplt = pastCookie.split("~");
                    var len = pastSearchSplt.length-1;                                 
                    for (i = len; i >= 0; i--) {
                        innerPastsplt = pastSearchSplt[i].split("|");
                        valToBindSplt = innerPastsplt[1].split("^");

                        if (valToBindSplt.length > -1) {

                            stringToShow += "<li class='airport'>";
                            stringToShow += "<span class='sector'>" + valToBindSplt[12] + " > " + valToBindSplt[13] + ", " + "</span>";

                            stdate = valToBindSplt[9].split('-');

                            if (valToBindSplt[1] != "") {
                                endate = valToBindSplt[1].split('-');
                            }

                            if (valToBindSplt[1] == "") {
                                //stringToShow += "<span class='other-info'>" + stdate[0] + " " + stdate[1] + ", " + valToBindSplt[0].toUpperCase() + "</span>";
                                stringToShow += "<span class='other-info'>" + stdate[0] + " " + stdate[1] + "</span>";
                            }
                            else {
                                stringToShow += "<span class='other-info'>" + stdate[0] + " " + stdate[1] + " - " + endate[0] + " " + endate[1] + "</span>";
                            }

                            stringToShow += "<span class='sr-only'>" + innerPastsplt[1] + "</span>";
                            stringToShow += "<span class='sr-onlypayselect'>" + valToBindSplt[14] + "^" + valToBindSplt[15] + "^" + valToBindSplt[16] + "^" + valToBindSplt[17] + "</span>";
                            stringToShow += "</li>";

                        }

                    }
                    stringToShow += "</ul>";
                    $("h3[id$='lblDest']").hide();
                    $("div[id$='dvPastSearch']").html(stringToShow);

                }
            }
            else {
                var ul = $("ul.past-searches")[0];
                if ($(ul).children().length <= 0) {
                    $(ul).prev().hide();
                }

            }
        }

        
        $(document).ready(function () {            
            BindRVOBECookie();            
            $("a[id$='lnkFlightsNHotels']").attr('onclick', setDataLayer('Flights-hotels', 'Home-BookOnline'));
            nearestAirCookie = getCookie("NearestAirport");
            if (nearestAirCookie != "" || nearestAirCookie != null) {
                aircodesplt = nearestAirCookie.split('=');
                if (aircodesplt.length > 0) {
                    aircode = aircodesplt[1];
                }
            }

            GetBestFares(aircode, $("div[id*='ObeBestFaresFrom']"));
            $("div[id*='ObeBestFaresTo']").html($("div[id*='ObeBestFaresFrom']").html());

            var BaseLanguageCode = 'EN';
            var BaseCountryCode = 'IN';
            var chkIAF = $("input[id$='chkIndianArmedForces']");
            if (BaseLanguageCode.toUpperCase() == "EN" && BaseCountryCode.toUpperCase() == "IN") {
                if ($(chkIAF).length > 0) {
                    $(chkIAF).closest('div').show();
                }
            }
            else {
                if ($(chkIAF).length > 0) {
                    $(chkIAF).closest('div').hide();
                }
            }

            var siaC = "";
            var siaparamC = "";
            var siaSplitC = "";
            var mobAppVal = "false";
            if (SIACookie != undefined && SIACookie != "") {

                siaSplitC = SIACookie.split('&');
                if (siaSplitC.length > 1) {

                    siaC = siaSplitC[0];
                    siaparamC = siaC.split('=');
                    if (siaparamC.length > 1 && siaparamC[1].toLowerCase() == "y") {
                        mobAppVal = "true";
                    }
                }
            }

            var $modal_Clone = $("#submit-confirm").clone(true);
            $("#submit-confirm").remove();
            $("form").append($modal_Clone);


            var mobForMobBrowser = "";
            dtype = device.mobile();


            if (dtype == true) {
                mobForMobBrowser = "mob";
            }

            var multilnk = $("a[id$='lnkMultipleDests']");
            if (mobAppVal == "true") {
                $(multilnk).attr('href', multilnk.attr('href') + '&mobApp=true' + '&origin=' + BaseCountryCode + "&lang=" + BaseLanguageCode + "&mobBrw=false");
            }
            else {
                if (mobForMobBrowser.toLowerCase() == "mob") {
                    $(multilnk).attr('href', multilnk.attr('href') + '&mobApp=false' + '&origin=' + BaseCountryCode + "&lang=" + BaseLanguageCode + "&mobBrw=true");
                }
                else {
                    $(multilnk).attr('href', multilnk.attr('href') + '&mobApp=false' + '&origin=' + BaseCountryCode + "&lang=" + BaseLanguageCode + "&mobBrw=false");
                }
            }

            var fltNhotel = $("a[id$='lnkFlightsNHotels']");
            $(fltNhotel).attr('href', fltNhotel.attr('href') + BaseCountryCode);
            

            $("button[id$='btnBookOnline']").click(function (e) {                
                var submitVal = document.getElementById("SubmitStateObeRev").value;
                if (submitVal == "true") {
                    RedirectURLObeRev("OnlineBookingForPastSearches",e);
                    return false;
                }

            });


            $("li[id$='Cash']").click(function () {

                var functionCallfrom = $(this).attr('class').split(' ')[1];
                $past = $("div[id$='dvOBEDefault']").text().replace('<ul class="airport-list past-searches">', "");

            $("li[id$='Miles']").click(function () {
                
                var functionCallfrom = $(this).attr('class').split(' ')[1];
                if (pastCookie == undefined || pastCookie == "") {
                    $past = $("div[id$='dvRBEDefault']").text().replace('<ul class="airport-list past-searches">', "");
                    $past = $past.replace('</ul>', "");
                    $(".past-searches").html($past);
                }


                if ($("input[id$='autoOrigin_AutoText']").val() != "" || $("input[id$='autoDestination_AutoText']").val() != "") {

                    var isAvail = CheckifOptionAvailable("miles");
                    if (isAvail == "false") {
                        JET.showMessage("info", $("label[id$='lblPaySwapMsghome']").html());
                    }
                    else if (isAvail.toLowerCase().indexOf("not eligible to redeem") > -1) {
                        JET.showMessage("error", isAvail);
                    }
                    else {
                    }
                }
            });

            $("li[id$='liCashNMiles']").click(function () {

                var functionCallfrom = $(this).attr('class').split(' ')[1];
                $past = $("div[id$='dvCNMDefault']").text().replace('<ul class="airport-list past-searches">', "");
                $past = $past.replace('</ul>', "");
                $(".past-searches").html($past);
                if ($("input[id$='autoOrigin_AutoText']").val() != "" || $("input[id$='autoDestination_AutoText']").val() != "") {

                    var isAvail = CheckifOptionAvailable("cash-miles");
                    if (isAvail == "false") {
                        JET.showMessage("info", $("label[id$='lblPaySwapMsghome']").html());
                    }
                    else {
                    }

                }
            });



            if ($("label[id$='lblDownMsg']").html() != "") {
                $("#oneWay_trigger").closest('span').addClass('is-disabled');
                $("#roundTrip__trigger").closest('span').addClass('is-disabled');
                $("#noOfTravellers").val(1);
                $('.close').hide();

                ShowMessage("error", $("label[id$='lblDownMsg']").html());
            }

            $("div[id$='pnlDownTimeMessage']").hide();

                e.preventDefault();

                $("#hdnLoginPopup").trigger("click");
            });

            if (adultreq == "") {
                $("select[id$='ddlAdult']").val(1);
            }

            if (childreq == "") {
                $("select[id$='ddlChildren']").val(0);
            }

            if (infantreq == "") {
                $("select[id$='ddlInfant']").val(0);

                    $(".flight-ret-date").addClass("is-oneway");

                if ($("input[id$='txtStartDate']").val().indexOf(',') > -1) {
                    var stDate = $("input[id$='txtStartDate']").val().replace(" ", "-").replace(",", "-").split("-");

                    var edDate = "";
                    if ($("input[id$='txtEndDate']").val().indexOf(',') > -1) {
                        edDate = $("input[id$='txtEndDate']").val().replace(" ", "-").replace(",", "-").split("-");
                    }

                    var newStartDate = new Date("20" + stDate[2].trim(), monthsList.indexOf(stDate[1]), stDate[0].trim());

                    var newEndDate = new Date();
                    if (edDate.length > 2) {

                        newEndDate = new Date("20" + edDate[2].trim(), monthsList.indexOf(edDate[1]), edDate[0].trim());
                    }

                    if ($("input[id$='txtStartDate']").val() != "") {
                        $("input[id$='txtStartDate']").val(stDate[0] + ' ' + stDate[1] + ',' + stDate[2].trim());
                    }
                    else {
                        $("input[id$='txtStartDate']").val($("input[id$='hdnDepart']").val());
                    }

                    if ($("input[id$='txtEndDate']").val() != "" && edDate.length > 2) {
                        $("input[id$='txtEndDate']").val(edDate[0] + ' ' + edDate[1] + ',' + edDate[2].trim());
                    }
                    else {
                        $("input[id$='txtEndDate']").val($("input[id$='hdnReturn']").val());
                    }
                    $("#departureCalendar").datepicker("setDate", newStartDate);
                    $("#returnCalendar").datepicker("setDate", newEndDate);
                } else {
                    $("input[id$='txtStartDate']").val($("input[id$='hdnDepart']").val());
                    $("input[id$='txtEndDate']").val($("input[id$='hdnReturn']").val());
                }

            }
            JET.bookingWidget._modifyInfantsDropdowns();
        });

        function CheckifOptionAvailable(option) {

            var optFlag = "false";
            var originPaySelection;
            var destPaySelection;

            if ($("input[id$='hdnOriginPaySelection']").val().indexOf('^') > -1) {
                originPaySelection = $("input[id$='hdnOriginPaySelection']").val().split('^');
                destPaySelection = $("input[id$='hdnDestPaySelection']").val().split('^');
            }
            else {
                originPaySelection = $("input[id$='hdnOriginPaySelection']").val();
                destPaySelection = $("input[id$='hdnDestPaySelection']").val();
            }

            var optOriMile = "";
            var optOriCNM = "";
            var optDestMile = "";
            var optDestCNM = "";

            if (originPaySelection.length > 0) {
                optOriMile = originPaySelection[1].split(':')[1];
                optOriCNM = originPaySelection[2].split(':')[1];
                optDestMile = destPaySelection[1].split(':')[1];
                optDestCNM = destPaySelection[2].split(':')[1];
            }

            var chkAirport = "";
            if (optOriMile == "" || optDestMile == "") {
                chkAirport = ChkPaySelectionForAirportsOnPastSearchONChange($("input[id$='hdnAutoOriginValue']").val(), $("input[id$='hdnAutoDestinationValue']").val(), "miles");

                if (chkAirport.toLowerCase() == "y") {
                    optFlag = "true";
                }
                else if (chkAirport.toLowerCase().indexOf("not eligible to redeem") > -1) {
                    optFlag = chkAirport;
                }
                else {
                    optFlag = "false";
                }

            }
            else {
                if (option == "miles") {
                    if (optOriMile.toLowerCase() == "y" && optDestMile.toLowerCase() == "y") {
                        optFlag = "true";
                    }
                }

                if (option == "cash-miles") {
                    if (optOriCNM.toLowerCase() == "y" && optDestCNM.toLowerCase() == "y") {
                        optFlag = "true";
                    }
                }
            }
            return optFlag;
        }

        function ResetTxt() {
            $(originToReset).val("");
            $(hdnOriginToReset).val("");
            $(hdnUntrimedOriginToReset).val("");
            $(destinationToReset).val("");
            $(hdnDestinationToReset).val("");
            $(hdnUntrimedDestinationToReset).val("");
            $(hdnOriginPaySelectionToReset).val("");
            $(hdnDestPaySelectionToReset).val("");
        }

        function removeError(id) {
            $("#" + id).closest('.frm__control').removeClass('has-error');
        }

        function GetParameterValues(param) {
            var retParam = "";
            var url = window.location.href.slice(window.location.href.indexOf('?') + 1).split('&');
            for (var i = 0; i < url.length; i++) {
                var urlparam = url[i].split('=');
                if (urlparam[0] == param) {
                    retParam = urlparam[1];
                }
            }
            return retParam;
        }


        function RedirectURLObeRev(postControl,btnEvent) {            
            
            var CC_CODE = 'IN';
            if ((CC_CODE).toLowerCase() === "in") {
                $("input[id$='chkWomenDayOffer']").parent().show();
                $("span[id$='lblWomenDayOffer']").show();
            }

            var btnBookOnline = $("input[id$='btnBookOnline']");
            var ReturnPromoCode = 'promocode';
            var ObePinStrom = '';


            var PromoCode = ""; var message = null;
            if ($('#ObeFlights1_txtPromotion').val() != 'Optional')
                PromoCode = $('#ObeFlights1_txtPromotion').val();
            else {
                if (document.getElementById('hdnADQueryStringParameter') != null) {
                    PromoCode = document.getElementById('hdnADQueryStringParameter').value;
                }
            }

            var searchBy = "";

            var tripType = true;
            var $retDate = $('input[id$="txtEndDate"]').parent().parent();
            if ($retDate.hasClass('is-oneway')) {
                tripType = false;
            }

            if ($('input[id$=txtEndDate]').val() == "One Way") {
                tripType = false;
            }

            var currentPaySelection = $('.selection').parent().find('span').attr('class').split(' ')[1];
            var paySelection = "Cash:^Miles:^CashNMiles:^PaySelect:" + currentPaySelection;
            var wdo = $("input[id$='chkWomenDayOffer']").is(':checked') || false;

            var srcmode = GetSRCMode(currentPaySelection);
            var device = GetDevice();

            var browser = GetBrowser();
            var deviceId = "";
            var mobApp = "false";
            var muserip = "";
            var musercountry = "";
            var mobBrw = "false";

            var ShowInAppCookie = getCookie("ShowInApp");
            var sia = "";
            var siaparam = "";
            var siaSplit = "";

            var deviceparam = "";
            var deviceIdparam = "";
            var mucntyparam = "";

            if (ShowInAppCookie != undefined && ShowInAppCookie != "") {

                siaSplit = ShowInAppCookie.split('&');
                if (siaSplit.length > 1) {

                    sia = siaSplit[0];
                    device = siaSplit[1];
                    deviceId = siaSplit[2];
                    musercountry = siaSplit[3];

                    siaparam = sia.split('=');
                    if (siaparam.length > 1 && siaparam[1].toLowerCase() == "y") {
                        mobApp = "true";
                        mobBrw = "false";
                    }

                    if (mobApp == "true") {
                        if (deviceId.indexOf("=") > 0) {
                            deviceIdparam = deviceId.split('=');
                            if (deviceIdparam.length > 1) {
                                deviceId = deviceIdparam[1];
                            }
                        }

                        if (device.indexOf("=") > 0) {
                            deviceparam = device.split('=');
                            if (deviceparam.length > 1) {
                                device = deviceparam[1];
                            }
                        }

                        mucntyparam = musercountry.split('=');
                        if (mucntyparam.length > 1) {
                            musercountry = mucntyparam[1];
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

            if (dtype == true) {
                mobBrw = "true";
                if (currentPaySelection.toLowerCase() == "cash") {
                    srcmode = "MOB";
                }
                if (currentPaySelection.toLowerCase() == "miles") {
                    srcmode = "RBE";
                }
            }


            if (mobApp == "true" && currentPaySelection.toLowerCase() != "miles") {
                srcmode = "MOB";
            }

            if (mobApp == "true" && currentPaySelection.toLowerCase() == "miles") {
                srcmode = "RBE";
            }

            var untrimedOrigin = "";
            var untrimedDestination = "";

            var originText = $("input[id*='autoOrigin']").val();
            var destinationText = $("input[id*='autoDestination']").val();

            if (originText.indexOf("...") > 0) {
                originText = $("input[id$='hdnUntrimedOrigin']").val();
            }

            if (destinationText.indexOf("...") > 0) {
                destinationText = $("input[id$='hdnUntrimedDestination']").val();
            }

            var hdnOri = $("input[id$='hdnAutoOriginValue']").val();
            var hdnDest = $("input[id$='hdnAutoDestinationValue']").val();

            var isIAF = $("input[id$='chkIndianArmedForces']").is(':checked') || false;
            var isReturn = $("inputxtEndDateValt[id$='hdnPromoAccepted']").val();

            

            var txtEndDateVal = $('#ObeFlights1_txtEndDate').val();
            var ddlAdultVal = $('#ObeFlights1_ddlAdult').val();
            var ddlChildrenVal = $('#ObeFlights1_ddlChildren').val();
            var ddlInfantVal = $('#ObeFlights1_ddlInfant').val();
            var txtStartDateVal = $('#ObeFlights1_txtStartDate').val();

            var txtEndDateVaToSend = "";
            if (txtEndDateVal.indexOf(",") > -1) {
                txtEndDateVaToSend = txtEndDateVal;
            }
            

            var source = "";
            if (currentPaySelection.toLowerCase() == "cash") {
                source = "HomeOBE";
            }
            else if (currentPaySelection.toLowerCase() == "miles") {
                source = "HomeOBE";
                srcmode = "RBE";
            }
            else {
            }                       
            if (mobApp == "true") { mobBrw = "false"; }

            $.post("/JQueryAddUserControl.aspx",
            {
                ClickedControl: postControl,
                RoundTrip: (tripType || false),
                EndDate: txtEndDateVaToSend,
                Adult: ddlAdultVal,
                Children: ddlChildrenVal,
                Infant: ddlInfantVal,
                Origin: hdnOri,
                Destination: hdnDest,
                OriginText: originText,
                DestinationText: destinationText,
                StartDate: txtStartDateVal,
                FixedDates: searchBy,
                Promotion: PromoCode,
                PastSearchText: '',
                SearchBy: searchBy,
                IAF: isIAF,
                IsReturn: isReturn,
                Source: source,
                WDO: wdo,
                PinStrom: ObePinStrom,
                PaySelection: paySelection,
                SRCMode: srcmode,
                Device: device,
                Browser: browser,
                DeviceId: deviceId,
                MobApp: mobApp,
                Muip: muserip,
                Musercountry: musercountry,
                MobBrw: mobBrw
            }, function (data) {

                var redirectURL = data;
                if (data == "FlightNotAvailable") {
                    JET.showMessage("info", "Flight Not Available");
                    return false;
                }


                var redirectURLSplit = redirectURL.split('$^');

                var returnValue = true;

                message = redirectURLSplit[1];
                var promoFlag;
                var URL;
                var isPromoAccepted = $("input[id$='hdnPromoAccepted']").val(); //Syntax error fixed.
                var isReturnTrip = ($('#ObeFlights1_Return').prop('checked') || false);
                if (message) {

                    if (message.indexOf('$$') != -1) {
                        promoFlag = message.split('$$')[1];
                        message = message.split('$$')[0];
                    }
                }
                if (postControl == "OnlineBookingForPastSearches") {
                    if (redirectURLSplit[0] == "StopFlow") {
                        if (redirectURLSplit.length == 2) {
                            JET.showMessage("error", redirectURLSplit[1]);
                        }
                        else {
                            if (redirectURLSplit[4].toLowerCase() == "alert") {
                                //alert(message);
                                JetConfirm($("button[id$='btnBookOnline']"), "Flight Search", message, "alert", btnEvent,"#booking");
                                returnValue = flc;
                                flc = false;
                            }
                            else {
                                //confirm(message);
                                JetConfirm($("button[id$='btnBookOnline']"), "Flight Search", message, "confirm", btnEvent, "#booking");
                                returnValue = flc;
                                flc = false;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    else {
                        if (redirectURLSplit[1] != "") {
                            if (redirectURLSplit[4].toLowerCase() == "htmlpopup") {
                                var startdate = $('#ObeFlights1_txtStartDate').val();
                                var startdatearr = startdate.split('-');

                                startdatearr[1] = getMonthNumber(startdatearr[1]) - 1
                                var tomorrow = new Date();
                                tomorrow.setDate(tomorrow.getDate() + 331);
                                var endDay = tomorrow.getDate();
                                var endMonth = tomorrow.getMonth();
                                var endYear = tomorrow.getFullYear();

                                var message = redirectURLSplit[1];
                                message = message.replace('document.getElementById("txtReturnDate"), new Date(), new Date()', 'document.getElementById("txtReturnDate"), new Date(' + startdatearr[2] + ',' + startdatearr[1] + ',' + startdatearr[0] + '), new Date(' + endYear + ',' + endMonth + ',' + endDay + ')');
                                message = message.replace('document.getElementById("txtReturnDate"), new Date(), new Date()', 'document.getElementById("txtReturnDate"), new Date(' + startdatearr[2] + ',' + startdatearr[1] + ',' + startdatearr[0] + '), new Date(' + endYear + ',' + endMonth + ',' + endDay + ')');
                                $('#PopUPReplace').append(message);

                                $('.LoginTabImg, .LoginTabImgPRS').css({ zIndex: '800' });

                            }
                            else if (redirectURLSplit[4].toLowerCase() == "alert") {
                                //alert(message);
                                JetConfirm($("button[id$='btnBookOnline']"), "Flight Search", message, "alert", btnEvent, "#booking");
                                returnValue = flc;
                                flc = false;                                
                            }
                            else {
                                //returnValue = confirm(message);                                
                                JetConfirm($("button[id$='btnBookOnline']"), "Flight Search", message, "confirm", btnEvent, "#booking");
                                    returnValue = flc;
                                    flc = false;                                    
                            }
                        }
                        if (redirectURLSplit[2] == "RedirectGetMethod" && redirectURLSplit[4].toLowerCase() != "htmlpopup") {
                            var stdt = "";
                            var rtdt = "";
                            if (returnValue) {

                                URL = redirectURLSplit[3];
                                originText = originText.replace(originText.substring(originText.indexOf('('), originText.length), "").trim();
                                destinationText = destinationText.replace(destinationText.substring(destinationText.indexOf('('), destinationText.length), "").trim();

                                var stdtsplt = txtStartDateVal.replace(',', "/").replace(' ', '/').split('/');

                                var stmonth = "";
                                stmonth = getMonthNumber(stdtsplt[1]);
                                if (stmonth.toString().length < 2) {
                                    stmonth = "0" + stmonth;
                                }

                                stdt = stdtsplt[0].trim() + "/" + stmonth + "/" + "20" + stdtsplt[2].trim();


                                //var rtdtsplt = txtEndDateVal.replace(',', "/").replace(' ', '/').split('/');
                                //var edmonth = getMonthNumber(rtdtsplt[1]);
                                //if (edmonth.toString().length < 2) {
                                //    edmonth = "0" + edmonth;
                                //}

                                //rtdt = rtdtsplt[0].trim() + "/" + edmonth + "/" + "20" + rtdtsplt[2].trim();

                                //if (tripType) {
                                //}
                                //else {
                                //    rtdt = "";
                                //}


                                var edmonth = "";
                                var rtdtsplt = "";
                                if (txtEndDateVal.indexOf(',') > -1) {

                                    rtdtsplt = txtEndDateVal.replace(',', "/").replace(' ', '/').split('/');
                                    edmonth = getMonthNumber(rtdtsplt[1]);
                                    if (edmonth.toString().length < 2) {
                                        edmonth = "0" + edmonth;
                                    }

                                    rtdt = rtdtsplt[0].trim() + "/" + edmonth + "/" + "20" + rtdtsplt[2].trim();

                                    if (tripType) {
                                    }
                                    else {
                                        rtdt = "";
                                    }
                                }

                                var strtoCompare = "/Process/RedeemLanding.aspx";
                                strtoCompare = strtoCompare.toLowerCase(strtoCompare);
                                if (URL.toLowerCase().indexOf(strtoCompare) > -1) {
                                    setDataLayer('Miles', 'Header');
                                    window.location.href = URL + "&from=" + originText + "&to=" + destinationText + "&departdate=" + stdt + "&returndate=" + rtdt;
                                    return false;
                                }
                                else {
                                    setDataLayer('Cash', 'Header');
                                    window.location.href = "searchingflights.aspx?param=" + URL + "&from=" + originText + "&to=" + destinationText + "&departdate=" + stdt + "&returndate=" + rtdt;
                                    return false;
                                }
                            }
                            else {
                                if (redirectURLSplit[5] == "ReturnDiscount" && redirectURLSplit[4].toLowerCase() != "htmlpopup") {
                                    if (redirectURLSplit[6] == "true" && promoFlag == "ReturnPromo") {
                                        $("input[id$='hdnPromoAccepted']").val('true');//Syntax error fixed
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                        else if (redirectURLSplit[2] == "RedirectGetMethodEtihad" && redirectURLSplit[4].toLowerCase() != "htmlpopup") {
                            if (returnValue) {
                                $.colorbox({
                                    inline: true,
                                    width: "500px",
                                    height: "250px",
                                    opacity: "0.85",
                                    transition: "fade",
                                    escKey: false,
                                    closeButton: false,
                                    href: "#popUpBRD",
                                    onComplete: function () {
                                        $("#popUpBRD").css('display', 'block');
                                        $("#cboxClose").css('display', 'none');

                                        $('#RBDok').live('click', function () {
                                            proceed = true;
                                            URL = redirectURLSplit[3];
                                            window.location.href = URL;
                                            $.colorbox.close();
                                        });
                                        $('#RBDcancel').live('click', function () {
                                            proceed = false;
                                            $.colorbox.close();
                                        });
                                    },
                                    onCleanup: function () {
                                        $('#popUpBRD').css('display', 'none');
                                    }
                                });
                            }
                            else {
                                if (redirectURLSplit[5] == "ReturnDiscount" && redirectURLSplit[4].toLowerCase() != "htmlpopup") {
                                    if (redirectURLSplit[6] == "true" && promoFlag == "ReturnPromo") {
                                        $("input[id$='hdnPromoAccepted']").val('true');//Syntax Error Fixed
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                else {
                    if (redirectURLSplit[0] == "RedirectGetMethod") {
                        window.location.href = redirectURLSplit[1];
                        //$(".loading").hide();
                    }
                    else if (redirectURLSplit[0] == "RedirectGetMethodEtihad") {
                        window.location.href = redirectURLSplit[1];
                        //$(".loading").hide();
                    }                    
                    else if (redirectURLSplit[0] == "PastSearch") {
                        populateValues(redirectURLSplit[1]);
                        //$(".loading").hide();
                    }
                    else if (redirectURLSplit[0] == "RedirectPostMethod") {
                    }
                }
            });

            return false;
        }
        function populateValues(data1) {


            var txtOriginID = $('input[id*="autoOrigin"]');
            var txtDestID = $('input[id*="autoDestination"]');
            var ddlOri = $('input[id$="hdnAutoOriginValue"]');
            var ddlDest = $('input[id$="hdnAutoDestinationValue"]');

            var rdoOneWay = "ObeFlights1_OneWay";
            var rdoRoundTrip = "ObeFlights1_Return";
            var rdoFixedDates = "";
            var rdoFlexibleDates = "";
            var rdoLowestFares = "";

            var ddlAdult = "ObeFlights1_ddlAdult";
            var ddlChildren = "ObeFlights1_ddlChildren";
            var ddlInfant = "ObeFlights1_ddlInfant";
            var txtEndDate = "ObeFlights1_txtEndDate";
            var txtStartDate = "ObeFlights1_txtStartDate";
            var txtPromotion = "ObeFlights1_txtPromotion";
            var btnEndDateCal = "";

            var ddlSearchBy = "";
            var countryCode = "IN";

            populateValuesOBESearchBy(data1, txtOriginID, txtDestID, ddlOri, ddlDest, rdoOneWay, rdoRoundTrip, ddlSearchBy, ddlAdult, ddlChildren, ddlInfant, txtEndDate, txtStartDate, txtPromotion, btnEndDateCal, countryCode);
        }

    </script>



</div>

    <script>
        $(document).ready(function () {
            var arrNews = NewsArray;
            var lstNews;
            if (NoNews == true) {
                $("#fscroller").html('No news updates available.');
            }
            else {
                /* just testing from front end.
                arrNews.push("<a data-file='/PressReleases/2015_01_30.txt' class='newsLink' href='#newsPopup' aria-controls='newsPopup' aria-expanded='false' data-toggle='modal'>Sample Link for Popup</a>");*/
                $("#fscroller").html(arrNews);
                lstNews = $("#fscroller a");
                do {
                    $(lstNews.slice(0, 3)).wrapAll('<li />');
                }
                while ((lstNews = lstNews.slice(3)).length > 0)

                $('.news-slider').on('click', '.newsLink', function (e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    $('.loading').show();
                    loadPress($(this).attr("data-file"));
                });

            }

            //Modal pop-up code - start
            var $modal_Clone_newsPopup;
            $modal_Clone_newsPopup = $("#newsPopup").clone(true);
            $("#newsPopup").remove();
            $("form").append($modal_Clone_newsPopup);
            //Modal pop-up code - end
        });

        function loadPress(PressUrl) {
            $("#pressReleaseBody").html("");
            $("#pressReleaseBody").load(PressUrl, function (response, status, xhr) {
                if (status == "success") {
                    //Loaded sucess    
                    $('.loading').hide();
                }
                else {
                    //Not Loaded 
                    $('.loading').hide();
                }
            });
        }
    </script>

    <script type="text/javascript">

        $(document).ready(function () {
            var childLiLen;
            var $originalLi;
            var finalList = "";
            var lastLiCount = 0;
            var constCount = 0;
            var lastLiCountStep = 0;
            var liGroup = new Array();
            var col = i = 0;

            $('div.tab__container').find('.tab__content').each(function () {
                childLiLen = $(this).find('.cities > li').length;
                constCount = childLiLen / 3;
                lastLiCount = constCount;
                if (childLiLen > 20) {
                    $originalLi = $(this).find('.cities > li');
                    for (col = 0; col < 3; col++) {
                        finalList += "<ul class='cities'>";
                        liGroup = $originalLi.slice(lastLiCountStep, lastLiCount);
                        for (i = 0; i < liGroup.length; i++) {
                            finalList += liGroup[i].outerHTML;
                        }
                        finalList += "</ul>";
                        lastLiCountStep = (lastLiCount);
                        lastLiCount += constCount;
                    }
                    $(this).html('');
                    $(this).append(finalList);
                }
                finalList = "";
                lastLiCount = 0;
                constCount = 0;
                lastLiCountStep = 0;

            });

            $('div.tab-headers').find('ul.tab__head').find("li:eq(0)").trigger('click');
            $('#ToC li:first a').addClass('active');
            $('.tab__container div:first').addClass('active');

        });
    </script>

        $(document).ready(function () {

        function ChangeCheckedValue(chkRemeberMe) {
            chkRemeberMe.value = (chkRemeberMe.checked) ? "on" : "off";
        }

        //setRememberMeLoginCookie('popup');

        function checkCookieRm() {
            var JPNumberRm;
            var CurrentSiteInfoRm = getCookie(JPNumberRm);
            if (CurrentSiteInfoRm !== null && CurrentSiteInfoRm !== "") {
                document.getElementById("LoginPop_chkRemeberMe").checked = true;
            }
            else {
                document.getElementById("LoginPop_chkRemeberMe").checked = false;
            }
        }

        function ValidateAndRedirect() {
            var msgWithFlagPop = new Array();
            msgWithFlagPop[0] = "";
            msgWithFlagPop[1] = "error";
            var hdnAutoOriginValueObj = $("input[id$='hdnAutoOriginValue']").val();
            var hdnAutoDestinationValueObj = $("input[id$='hdnAutoDestinationValue']").val();
            var SubmitStatus = document.getElementById("SubmitStateObeRev");

            //calling this function ti check eligibility of redemption  - CheckPaySelectionForAirportsOnPastSearch
            //msgWithFlagPop = CheckPaySelectionForAirportsOnPastSearch($("input[id$='hdnAutoOriginValue']").val(), $("input[id$='hdnAutoDestinationValue']").val(), "miles", "bookbtn")
            msgWithFlagPop = CheckPaySelectionForAirportsOnPastSearch(hdnAutoOriginValueObj, hdnAutoDestinationValueObj, "miles", "bookbtn");
            /*for (z = 0; z <= 40000; z++) {
                //Holding flow for 4 seconds.
            }*/
            if (msgWithFlagPop[0] != "") {
                $(".loading").hide();
                ShowMessage(msgWithFlagPop[1], msgWithFlagPop[0]);
                if (SubmitStatus) {
                    SubmitStatus.value = false;
                }
                return false;
            }
            else {
                $(".loading").hide();
                RedirectURLObeRev("OnlineBookingForPastSearches");
                //return false;
            }

        }

            var jpNumber = $('#LoginPop_txtJPNumber').val();
            var password = $('#LoginPop_txtPassword').val();

            var redemMsg = $("label[id$='lblEligibilityToRedeemMsg']").text();
            return CallByAuthenticateUserC(jpNumber, password, 'popup');
        }

        function getCookie(JetUserInfo) {
            if (document.cookie.length > 0) {
                c_start = document.cookie.indexOf(JetUserInfo + "=");

                //c_start=document.cookie
                if (c_start != -1) {
                    c_start = c_start + JetUserInfo.length + 1;
                    c_end = document.cookie.indexOf(";", c_start);
                    if (c_end == -1) c_end = document.cookie.length;
                    return unescape(document.cookie.substring(c_start, c_end));
                }
            }
            return "";
        }
